 2015 ke aankade ke anusaar in collejon main 16 lakh sattar hazaar seat hai

 unhone yah baat 2015 main kahi thi jo ek akhbaar main chhapi thi

 civil ejeeniyar ke liye sirf 6

 chemical dizine ejeeniyar ke kaam ke liye sabase kam 1
 Only 64% of engineers are qualified
 electronic ejeeniyar ke role ke liye 7

 aaj bahut se ejeeniyar chaar saal kii padhai ke baad paanch se das hazaar ke bich naukari karne par majaboor hai

 par honeymoon keval un donon ke liye hota he

 honeymoon par janaa isliye bhi jaruri hekhyonki ye wo vakt hota he jab do log ek-duusare par bharosa kaayam karte hai

 shaadi kaa matlab hi dhamal or masti se he

 2

 isse aapkaa do logon ke bich shaareerik or maansik lagaav badhata he

 3

 4
 shaadi ke baad pehali baar aap donon saath kahin ja rahe hai

 5
 There is exhaustion in the fight of marriage
 aise main honeymoon par janaa ek bahut acha idia he
 Returning from where you will feel absolutely fresh
